# [HCO] + Br- = [HCO]Br + e-
# add_logk HCO -1
# add_logk Br- -1
# add_logk e- 1
# add_logk Formylbromid 1
# [HCO] + I- = [HCO]I + e-
# add_logk HCO -1
# add_logk I- -1
# add_logk e- 1
# add_logk Formyljodid 1
# 2 [HCO] + [O] = [HCO]2[O]
# add_logk HCO -2
# add_logk O -1
# add_logk Formanhydrid 1
# [HCO] + [O] + [Me] = [HCO][O][Me]
# add_logk HCO -1
# add_logk O -1
# add_logk CH3 1
# add_logk Methyl-formiat 1
# [HCO] + [N][H]3 = [HCO][N][H]2 + [H]+ + e-
# add_logk HCO -1
# add_logk NH3 -1
# add_logk Formamid 1
# add_logk H+ 1
# add_logk e- 1
# [HCO] + [N_low][H]3 = [HCO][N_low][H]2 + [H]+ + e-
# add_logk HCO -1
# add_logk NH3 -1
# add_logk Formamid 1
# add_logk H+ 1
# add_logk e- 1
# [HCO] + [N_diaz][H]3 = [HCO][N_diaz][H]2 + [H]+ + e-
# add_logk HCO -1
# add_logk NH3 -1
# add_logk Formamid 1
# add_logk H+ 1
# add_logk e- 1
# [HCO] + [MeNH] = [HCO][MeNH]
# add_logk HCO -1
# add_logk MeNH -1
# add_logk N-Methylformamid 1
# [HCO] + [Me2N] = [HCO][Me2N]
# add_logk HCO -1
# add_logk Me2N -1
# add_logk N.N-Dimethylformamid 1

# [MeO] = [MeO]
# log_k 0
# [MeO] + [H]+ + e- = [MeO][H]
# add_logk MeO -1
# add_logk H+ -1
# add_logk e- -1
# add_logk Methanol
# [MeO][H] = [MeO]- + [H]+
# log_k -15.5
# #  Ballinger, P.; Long, F. A. (1960). "Acid Ionization Constants of Alcohols. II. Acidities of Some Substituted Methanols and Related Compounds". J. Am. Chem. Soc. 82 (4): 795–798. doi:10.1021/ja01489a008.
# [MeO] + [Me] = [MeO][Me]
# add_logk MeO -1
# add_logk CH3 -1
# add_logk Dimethylether 1
# 2 [MeO] = [MeO]2
# add_logk MeO -2
# add_logk Dimethylperoxid 1

# [MeS] = [MeS]
# log_k 0
# [MeS] + [H]+ + e- = [MeS][H]
# add_logk MeS -1
# add_logk H+ -1
# add_logk e- -1
# add_logk Methanthiol
# [MeS][H] = [MeS]- + [H]+
# log_k -10.4
# # https://hmdb.ca/metabolites/HMDB0003227
# [MeS] + [Me] = [MeS][Me]
# add_logk MeS -1
# add_logk CH3 -1
# add_logk Dimethylsulfid 1
# 2 [MeS] = [MeS]2
# add_logk MeS -2
# add_logk Dimethyldisulfid 1

# [MeN] = [MeN]
# log_k 0
# [MeN] + 3 [H]+ + 3 e- + [O] = [MeN][H]2[O][H]
# add_logk CH3N -1
# add_logk H+ -3
# add_logk e- -3
# add_logk O -1
# add_logk Methylhydroxylamin 1
# [MeN][H][O][H] + [H]+ = [MeN][H]2[O][H]+
# log_k 5.96
# # http://www.fm.ehcc.kyoto-u.ac.jp/pKa_compilation_Williams_RipinEvans.pdf
# [MeN] + [O] = [MeN][O]
# add_logk CH3N -1
# add_logk O -1
# add_logk Nitrosomethan 1
# [MeN] + 2 [O] = [MeN][O]2
# add_logk CH3N -1
# add_logk O -2
# add_logk Nitromethan 1

# [MeNH] = [MeNH]
# log_k 0
# [MeNH] + [H]+ + e- = [MeNH][H]
# add_logk MeNH -1
# add_logk H+ -1
# add_logk e- -1
# add_logk Methylamin 1
# [MeNH][H] + [H]+ = [MeNH][H]2+
# log_k 10.66
# # https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Methylamine

# [Me2N] = [Me2N]
# log_k 0
# [Me2N] + [H]+ + e- = [Me2N][H]
# add_logk Me2N -1
# add_logk H+ -1
# add_logk e- -1
# add_logk Dimethylamin 1
# [Me2N][H] + [H]+ = [Me2N][H]2+
# log_k 10.73
# # https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dimethylamine
# # [Me2N] + [Me] = [Me2N][Me]
# # add_logk Me2N -1
# # add_logk CH3 -1
# # add_logk Trimethylamin 1
# # [Me2N] + 2 [Me] = [Me2N][Me]2+ + e-
# # add_logk Me2N -1
# # add_logk CH3 -2
# # add_logk Tetramethylammonium+ 1
# # add_logk e- 1

# log_k 0
# [Me3N] + [H]+ = [Me3N][H]+
# log_k 9.80
# # https://pubchem.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/compound/Trimethylamine#section=Refractive-Index
# [Me3N] + [Me] = [Me3N][Me]+ + e-
# add_logk Trimethylamin -1
# add_logk CH3 -1
# add_logk Tetramethylammonium+ 1

# add_logk Trimethylamin -1
# add_logk O -1
# add_logk Trimethylamin-oxid 1
# [Me3N][O] + [H]+ = [Me3N][H][O]+
